Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists of Grand Prix Metz 2017
==========================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 26, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











The main event may have only started on Saturday morning, but the action already began on Friday. Naturally, we were most interested in the Last-Chance Trials run that day as those results actually influenced the Grand Prix itself, by awarding byes to all winners. Plus, their decklists showed the full range of possibilities available to resourceful people in this Limited environment, from blisteringly fast beatdown to multicolored control monstrosities ...







#### Pierre Duchesne, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
